# OpenAlternativeLearn

Open-source alternatives with Codex courses and interactive classrooms.

A curated awesome-list of open-source alternatives, extended with Codex HTML courses and interactive classroom previews.

Website: [https://open.aiflowlearn.net](https://open.aiflowlearn.net)

## AI & Machine Learning

### AI Development Platforms

| Project | Github Info | Alternative To | Codex \| Classroom |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| [Open Mercato](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/open-mercato) - A modular CRM/ERP framework built on Next.js and TypeScript that encodes hundreds of architectural decisions so dev teams can ship production features in days, not months. [Repo](https://github.com/open-mercato/open-mercato) | license: MIT; Star: 1.4K | SAP, Retool | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [Parlant](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/parlant) - A conversational AI server that manages agent behavior through context-aware guidelines, keeping responses consistent, auditable, and aligned at scale. [Repo](https://github.com/emcie-co/parlant) | license: Apache-2.0; Star: 18K | Voiceflow, Chatbase, Uchat | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [ACI.dev](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/aci-dev) - Platform for connecting AI agents to 500+ tools with built-in multi-tenant auth management and granular permissions using either function calling or a unified MCP server [Repo](https://github.com/aipotheosis-labs/aci) | license: Apache-2.0; Star: 4.8K | Pipedream, Eden AI, Rube | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [Agenta](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/agenta) - Open-source LLMOps platform providing prompt management, evaluation, and observability tools for building robust AI applications with team collaboration. [Repo](https://github.com/agenta-ai/agenta) | license: MIT; Star: 4.2K | LangSmith, Humanloop | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [AgentOS](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/agentos) - Open-source TypeScript runtime for autonomous AI agents with cognitive memory, multi-agent orchestration, runtime tool generation, and support for 21 LLM providers. [Repo](https://github.com/framersai/agentos) | license: Apache-2.0; Star: 576 | - | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [Agno](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/agno) - Open-source platform that enables developers to create, deploy and monitor AI agents with built-in memory, knowledge integration, and external tool connectivity. [Repo](https://github.com/agno-agi/agno) | license: Apache-2.0; Star: 41K | Kiro, LangChain, Humanloop | [Codex](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/agno-agi-agno) \| Coming soon |
| [Arize Phoenix](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/arize-phoenix) - Open-source platform for LLM tracing, evaluation, and optimization. Features automatic instrumentation, prompt playground, and real-time AI application monitoring. [Repo](https://github.com/arize-ai/phoenix) | license: Unknown; Star: 10K | LangSmith, LangChain, Humanloop | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [Beam](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/beam) - Run AI workloads with sub-second cold starts, elastic GPU scaling, and secure sandboxed environments. Scale to zero when idle, burst to thousands instantly. [Repo](https://github.com/beam-cloud/beta9/) | license: AGPL-3.0; Star: 1.7K | Together Sandbox, Vertex AI, Modal | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [Bifrost](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/bifrost) - Open-source AI gateway delivering 50x faster performance than alternatives. Access 1000+ models from 8+ providers with built-in governance, fallback, and observability. [Repo](https://github.com/maximhq/bifrost) | license: Apache-2.0; Star: 5.7K | Eden AI, OpenRouter, Vercel AI Gateway | [Codex](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/bifrost) \| Coming soon |
| [Botpress](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/botpress) - A comprehensive platform for creating AI agents with intuitive tools, extensive integrations, and enterprise-grade features powered by the latest language models. [Repo](https://github.com/botpress/botpress) | license: MIT; Star: 15K | Manychat, Voiceflow, Uchat | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [ByteChef](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/bytechef) - Create intelligent automation workflows combining AI agents with your favorite apps and services. Connect, automate, and scale your operations without complex coding. [Repo](https://github.com/bytechefhq/bytechef) | license: Unknown; Star: 773 | n8n, Make, Zapier | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [CodeZero](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/codezero) - Open-source no-code automation platform for logistics, chatbots, and AI agents. Deploy on cloud, self-host, or hybrid with complete data sovereignty and modular workflow design. [Repo](https://github.com/code0-tech/codezero) | license: Unknown; Star: 35 | Zoho Flow, Azure Logic Apps | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [CopilotKit](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/copilotkit) - Integrate production-ready AI copilots into any product quickly and easily with CopilotKit's open-source platform. [Repo](https://github.com/CopilotKit/CopilotKit) | license: MIT; Star: 35K | - | [Codex](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/copilotkit-copilotkit) \| Coming soon |
| [Daytona](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/daytona) - Elastic sandbox infrastructure for running AI-generated code with sub-90ms environment creation, stateful operations, and isolated execution across Python, TypeScript, Go, and more. [Repo](https://github.com/daytonaio/daytona/) | license: AGPL-3.0; Star: 72K | Together Sandbox, Modal, Sprites | [Codex](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/daytonaio-daytona) \| Coming soon |
| [Dify](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/dify) - Visual platform for building agentic workflows, RAG pipelines, and LLM-powered apps. Supports hundreds of models, MCP integration, and self-hosted deployment. [Repo](https://github.com/langgenius/dify) | license: Unknown; Star: 145K | Glide, Retool, Humanloop | [Codex](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/dify-llm-workflow-platform) \| [Classroom](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/classroom/dify) |
| [E2B](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/e2b) - Provide AI agents with secure, isolated sandboxes featuring real-world tools, code execution, and enterprise-grade security. Trusted by 88% of Fortune 100 companies. [Repo](https://github.com/e2b-dev/e2b) | license: Apache-2.0; Star: 13K | Together Sandbox, Modal, Sprites | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [Envoy AI Gateway](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/envoy-ai-gateway) - Open source gateway built on Envoy for routing application traffic to GenAI services. Supports 16+ LLM providers including OpenAI, Anthropic, AWS Bedrock. [Repo](https://github.com/envoyproxy/ai-gateway) | license: Apache-2.0; Star: 1.7K | Eden AI, Vercel AI Gateway, Cloudflare AI Gateway | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [FastGPT](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/fastgpt) - FastGPT is a free, open-source platform for creating AI-powered knowledge bases with data processing, model invocation, and visual workflows. [Repo](https://github.com/labring/fastgpt) | license: Unknown; Star: 28K | - | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [Flowise AI](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/flowise-ai) - Open source platform for building AI agents, chatbots, and multi-agent systems using a drag-and-drop interface, with support for 100+ LLMs and RAG. [Repo](https://github.com/flowiseai/flowise) | license: Apache-2.0; Star: 54K | n8n, Make, Power Apps | [Codex](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/flowiseai-flowise) \| [Classroom](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/classroom/flowise-ai) |
| [Giselle](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/giselle) - Create powerful AI agents using an intuitive node-based interface that connects multiple LLMs and data sources for automated documentation and development workflows. [Repo](https://github.com/giselles-ai/giselle) | license: Apache-2.0; Star: 534 | - | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [Grepture](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/grepture) - An AI gateway that sits on the request path to handle PII redaction, prompt injection blocking, tracing, evals, and cost tracking for OpenAI, Anthropic, and Gemini. [Repo](https://github.com/grepture/proxy) | license: AGPL-3.0; Star: 7 | Vercel AI Gateway, Cloudflare AI Gateway, Kong AI Gateway | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [Laminar](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/laminar) - Laminar is an open-source platform that helps collect, understand, and utilize data for building high-quality LLM applications. [Repo](https://github.com/lmnr-ai/lmnr) | license: Apache-2.0; Star: 3K | LangChain, Pinecone | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [Langflow](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/langflow) - Build, deploy, and iterate on AI agents, RAG applications, and MCP servers using a drag-and-drop visual interface backed by Python. [Repo](https://github.com/langflow-ai/langflow) | license: MIT; Star: 150K | - | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [Langfuse](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/langfuse) - Langfuse provides tracing, evaluations, prompt management, and analytics to debug and improve LLM applications. [Repo](https://github.com/langfuse/langfuse) | license: Unknown; Star: 29K | LangSmith, LangChain, Humanloop | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [Latitude](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/latitude) - Traces AI agents in production, automatically clusters failures into issues, generates evals from real failures, and alerts you when something breaks or regresses. [Repo](https://github.com/latitude-dev/latitude-llm) | license: MIT; Star: 4.1K | LangSmith, Humanloop, Weights | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [Letta](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/letta) - Letta is an open-source platform for creating AI agents with built-in memory, reasoning, and support for thousands of tools. [Repo](https://github.com/letta-ai/letta) | license: Apache-2.0; Star: 23K | Perplexity, LangChain, Pinecone | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [LibreChat](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/librechat) - Chat with multiple AI providers through a single self-hostable interface, with support for custom agents, file uploads, plugins, and multi-user access control. [Repo](https://github.com/danny-avila/librechat) | license: MIT; Star: 39K | Claude, Grok, ChatGPT | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [LiteLLM](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/litellm) - Acts as a unified proxy across 100+ LLMs, normalizing them to the OpenAI format while handling virtual keys, budgets, rate limits, fallbacks, and cost tracking. [Repo](https://github.com/berriai/litellm) | license: Unknown; Star: 50K | LangChain, Eden AI, OpenRouter | [Codex](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/berriai-litellm) \| Coming soon |
| [LLM Gateway](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/llm-gateway) - Route, manage, and analyze LLM requests across multiple providers with one API. Compatible with OpenAI format, includes usage analytics and performance monitoring. [Repo](https://github.com/theopenco/llmgateway) | license: MIT; Star: 1.3K | Eden AI, Vercel AI Gateway, Cloudflare AI Gateway | [Codex](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/llm-gateway) \| Coming soon |
| [LobeChat](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/lobechat) - A collaborative platform to create, schedule, and operate AI agents that handle long-running tasks, team workflows, and automated jobs without constant oversight. [Repo](https://github.com/lobehub/lobe-chat) | license: Unknown; Star: 79K | Claude, Grok, ChatGPT | [Codex](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/lobe-chat-multi-agent) \| Coming soon |
| [Mem0](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/mem0) - Adds persistent, searchable memory to AI agents and apps, so they remember user preferences and past interactions across sessions without pipeline changes. [Repo](https://github.com/mem0ai/mem0) | license: Apache-2.0; Star: 58K | LangChain, Pinecone, Vertex AI | [Codex](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/mem0-ai-memory-layer) \| [Classroom](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/classrooms/7bed9716-ba55-4442-b3f3-3cbb22343d0a) |
| [Milvus](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/milvus) - Open-source vector database optimized for similarity search, scaling to billions of vectors with minimal performance loss [Repo](https://github.com/milvus-io/milvus) | license: Apache-2.0; Star: 45K | Supabase, Pinecone, ElasticSearch | [Codex](https://www.aiflowlearn.net/codex/milvus-io-milvus) \| Coming soon |
| [Multica](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/multica) - Open-source platform that manages coding agents as team members, with task queues, skill libraries, runtime monitoring, and a unified activity feed. [Repo](https://github.com/multica-ai/multica) | license: Unknown; Star: 36K | - | Coming soon \| Coming soon |
| [Nango](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/nango) - Complete integrations platform with 500+ pre-built APIs, code-first approach, unified data models, and enterprise-grade security. Free tier available. | [OpenLIT](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/openlit) - Open-source observability platform for GenAI and LLM applications. Real-time monitoring, distributed tracing, prompt management, and AI model evaluation built on OpenTelemetry. | [Qdrant](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/qdrant) - Qdrant is an open-source vector database that provides high-performance similarity search for AI and machine learning applications. | [Rivet](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/rivet) - Open-source infrastructure for long-lived, in-memory processes called Actors. | [ILLA](https://open.aiflowlearn.net/illa) - Low-code platform allows you to build business apps, enables you to quickly create internal tools such as dashboard, crud app, admin panel, crm, cms, etc. Supports PostgreSQL, MySQL, Supabase, GraphQL, MongoDB, MSSQL, Rest API, Hugging Face, Redis, etc. Automate workflows with schedule or webhook. ## Built with AIFlowLearn

Each item can grow into a project detail page, a Codex architecture course, and an interactive classroom that carries the slide preview.
